posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:I booked the No. 1 and most expensive hotel on Ctrip during the May Day holiday, but it was not worth it. I will never stay there again. First of all, the hotel is located in a remote area, and it is not convenient to go anywhere. You can take the hotel shuttle bus. But the shuttle bus is not convenient, and it is infuriating to take the bus several times. You have to wait for 20 minutes for a 10-minute ride, and it is said to be a traffic jam. I looked at the navigation and there was no traffic jam at all. He just wanted to pick up more guests at one time and let you wait at the station in vain. There was not a single truth. The most infuriating thing was that on the second night, it was raining heavily. We walked to the designated pick-up point with difficulty. After waiting for more than 20 minutes, he called us to go to another station to take the bus, saying that the road was closed. But we saw cars coming and going at the place where we were waiting for the bus. He only thought about how to make it convenient for himself, and didn't care about the situation of the guests at all. In addition, the hotel's car can obviously go directly to the Meilu Villa scenic spot. When I asked the driver if he could go directly to the scenic spot, the driver deliberately didn't answer, and asked you to get off at one more station and then queue up to go back. I really can't understand how people with this mentality can provide good service?
There is no scenery from the hotel room.
The triple room only comes with two pairs of slippers. I took a hot shower, but the water became dirtier and dirtier halfway through (see the picture below) and there was no hot water in the end. It's a rip-off.
In short, it's not worth it. The attitude of the service staff is wrong. I won't stay here again.

msg:There are not many regular hotels to choose from in Lushan, so I finally chose this one. The advantages are that the room is large, the bed is moderately soft and hard, the bedding is comfortable, the service is good, and the breakfast is quite rich. Because there are many people staying during the May Day holiday, there was no water for showering at around 9 pm. I waited for more than half an hour for hot water to come, which is understandable. The next day, the staff sent a small tea set to express their apology. The hotel is more suitable for self-driving because it is a bit far from the central city. But it is convenient to have the hotel's own shuttle bus. It is better to come to Lushan in the off-season, and the experience will be better. I will come again if I have the chance.

After checking in, the housekeeper sister Huang Liping took me to the room, and introduced the hotel layout in a considerate way. After adding WeChat, she always provided considerate service.
The hotel package includes a dinner gift. I unreasonably asked to eat it separately for two days, and the front desk manager also actively found a way for me to solve it.

The most satisfactory thing is that I applied for a late check-out until 4 pm. After checking the room status, the front desk manager satisfied me and allowed me to take a short rest before leaving. I am really grateful.
In short, it is worth a five-star recommendation.
PS: It is nice to watch the sunset at the back of the hotel. Don't miss it if the weather is good~

msg:I rarely write reviews unless I encounter special people and things. This time I will make a special note: The hotel is in a valley on the top of the mountain, about 2.5-3 kilometers away from the central intersection of Guling Street (I walked there once). Daily travel mainly involves taking the hotel shuttle bus. But the advantage is that it is quiet and beautiful, and the scenery is beautiful at any time. I took photos of the daytime and nighttime scenery. At the same time, every service staff of the hotel is very warm and friendly, and they are always responsive, which reflects the high quality of a five-star hotel. When we arrived on the rainy day, the most enthusiastic and busy beautiful duty manager who got off the car and arranged for check-in and poured hot water, I didnâ€™t ask embarrassedly until I left the hotel if she was Wang Si (this name appears frequently in the comment area, it can be said to be famous), and it turned out to be the real person. And the girl Zhang Wanqing who took us to check in and sent us to the guest room was very quiet and had a beautiful smile. She was very nice. There are two handsome and gentle guys at the front desk. One of them is often consulted by me. He is very serious and patient. The other is more shy. Sorry, they usually don't stand outside the lobby counter. I can't see their name tags clearly, but I am very grateful. At the same time, I would like to thank everyone in the hotel for their enthusiastic service. Even the cleaning lady responded to the needs as soon as possible. Thank you.
I booked two days on Ctrip. It was rainy and foggy when I arrived. It was predicted that there would be snow in the future. The children made a fuss and waited for the snow. I stayed at the hotel for another night on the 6th. At night, I walked to the KFC in the town center by myself. There were various scenery on the road. There was no fog or rain on the mountain on the day I left (February 7). It was actually more suitable for taking pictures and wandering around, but Lushan also has a unique charm when it is foggy.
I will take a special note.
